name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:City Standard Room - Street-View (Double bed)
info:Stayed in November 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:1 Review
rating:2.5
posted:Posted December 3, 2023
msg:I stayed at this hotel for three nights in November 2023. It fell very short of my expectations. This is the worst hotel I have stayed in in China and one of the worst hotels I have stayed in ever. The only hotel where I have stayed that was worse was in Erdenet, Mongolia. I don't understand how there are so many good reviews. I question whether those who left good reviews actually stayed at the same hotel where I stayed.

1. The breakfast buffet was awful. The food was cold, stale, and seemed like it was left over from the previous day. When the juice and milk ran out, they were not refilled. The only Western breakfast selections were some stale pastries. I could barely stomach it. About the food being cold: When will Chinese restaurant managers finally learn that chafing dishes need to be heated from below in order to work properly? Just putting a heat lamp above the tray will not keep the food hot.

2. My non-smoking room smelled of cigarette smoke. Maybe it had been smoked in previously or maybe the smell was coming from the air vents. It wasn't a strong smell, but I could smell it. Also, the staff allowed guests to smoke in the lobby, despite this being against Chinese law.

3. The shower in the bathroom was difficult and dangerous to enter and exit, as the bathtub wall was too high.

4. There was a long hair stuck to the bathroom wall when I arrived and it remained there until I left.

5. The room was too hot. Opening the windows was useless because the windows only opened downward, so no cool air came in. (Hot air rises, cold air sinks. That's basic science.)

6. My reservation said I had two meals a day, breakfast and afternoon tea (16:00 to 18:00), but there was no afternoon tea.

7. There was an ice bucket in the room, but no ice machine. I was told to ask for ice from the restaurant during breakfast (which was also an ordeal--see no. 8), meaning you can only get ice before 10am.

8. Most of the staff spoke little to no English. I don't expect people in China to speak English, but I do expect the reception staff at a hotel chain which claims to be a chain of "international business hotels" to be able to speak English. The restaurant manager didn't even understand when I tried to tell her my room number for the included breakfast. She even asked a guest to translate for her. I was confused when said guest asked me, "What kind of breakfast do you want?" I was told to just tell the manager my room number.

I believe that the Radisson company should send some inspectors out to review this location, as it has certainly tarnished their reputation in my opinion.
----------------------------------------

Secondly, I booked a city street view room. I didn't expect that there would be any beautiful street view, but I didn't expect that I didn't even see the street, but the alley.

The above is to avoid thunder for everyone. To be honest, the hotel is really not worth the price.

msg:After a day trip to Tianjin, let‚Äôs talk about the Radisson Hotel Tianjin Aqua City where we stayed, the Radisson brand, owned by the Carlson Group. But the experience after check-in made me very disappointed. I feel that the price is much different from the expected experience. The reason for choosing an international joint brand hotel. It is nothing more than that the experience in service, facilities, and catering is stronger than others. It is a good plan to take my wife and children out for a day, find a comfortable hotel to rest for a night, and then return to Beijing the next day. But it does lead me to regret.
First talk about facilities and equipment:
1. The wallpaper in the room I live in is obviously cracked, and there are obvious traces of repairs. The repair skills of the engineers personally feel that they need to be improved.
2. The edge of the lampshade collapsed and a large pit was sunk, affecting the overall aesthetics of the room. The service personnel can restore it with a little handling, but it is still in the resale.
3. The TV signal in the room is poor, and the image is snowy and unclear.
Next, talk about room hygiene:
1. There is nothing wrong with the whole, but the sanitation in the dead corners is too poor. It can be seen that cleaning is missing. There are a few private area hairs hanging on the drain plug of the bathroom bathtub! Suppressing the nausea, I took it out to the washbasin and flushed down the water stopper. I still couldn't go down, and finally grabbed it with my hands. Disgusting home! Is the room hygiene of international brand hotels already so low? !
Let's talk about the room environment:
1. It is still a common air conditioning problem. If the temperature does not go up, the temperature set by the central unit will not give guests a comfortable and warm living environment. Blow the head of the bed directly from the outlet, and the temperature of the blown wind is higher than that of the natural wind. When I sleep at night, the wind blows out from the vent above me, and I am afraid that my family of three will be paralyzed. I had to turn off the air conditioner, and asked for an extra quilt to sleep warmer. Energy saving and consumption reduction also need to be determined according to the occupancy rate. Half of your house is occupied. Is it a bit unkind to control the energy in this area to pull back revenue?
The same goes for the restaurant, where I ate a breakfast in my coat. Nothing but cold.
Finally a word about the breakfast buffet:
1. The kitchen table is small and the moving lines are unreasonable. Therefore, the dishes are not rich, and they cannot be spread.
2. Five-star hotels (no? Not in use?) We don't know why. I didn't see a warming machine... The plate is cold, and the temperature of the food put on it drops quickly, so it's okay to eat quickly. If you eat slowly, it will cool down in no time.
3. The variety of dishes is not very rich, and the serving volume is very small. It was not the peak of dining at that time, and there were not many customers, but there were many empty plates. So the options for guests are reduced. Tube full for sure. Some dishes still taste good. But it is by no means enjoying the word. Enjoy a sumptuous five-star continental breakfast to start the day in a happy mood. This kind of thing can only appear in the promotional videos of the hotel's self-media, but actually don't even think about it.
The advantages of the hotel are as follows:
1. The location is super good. Downtown, next to a shopping mall.
2. After all, it is an international brand hotel, the etiquette and service initiative of the service staff is worthy of recognition. Road encounter etiquette is slightly better than domestic hotels. But at present, domestic brand hotels also emphasize the attention and service status of guests.
After I checked in, I found the cleanliness of the room and complained to the manager on duty that night. The hotel management staff's follow-up and feedback efficiency for guest complaints is still good. Sincere attitude and efficient service. But I personally think that no matter how good the service is, it is better to do a good job in basic service work first. Wouldn't it be nice to convert complementary services into creative ones? Reduce guest complaint rate and improve guest satisfaction. Isn't it better?
During the C/O the next day, report the problem of room air conditioning to the manager on duty the next day. And told the family of three to sleep all night with the cold, of course the manager on duty the day before said to change the room. But since all the things have been taken out, large and small piles, and a three-year-old child, it is too inconvenient to change. After all, it is a dead-end sanitation problem, and the hotel handles it conveniently. It is also troublesome to change rooms after tossing. But the air-conditioning problem at night troubled me a lot, and my daughter-in-law kept complaining about the bad hotel I chose. "Hate again" continued to be reflected on the hotel. The convenience of the hotel is still officially operated. neither warm nor hot. It doesn't matter. Perhaps now that the hotel industry has been dragged down by the epidemic for three years, its positioning has been pulled down more or less. Sadness for the industry as a whole.
